class="Bound">eq2</a> <a id="19227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#19202" class="Bound">z</a><a id="19228" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19231" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Two terms M and N are denotational equal when their denotations are
equal, that is, ℰ M ≃ ℰ N.


## Road map for the following chapters

The subsequent chapters prove that the denotational semantics has
several desirable properties. First, we prove that the semantics is
compositional, i.e., that the denotation of a term is a function of
the denotations of its subterms. To do this we shall prove equations
of the following shape.

    ℰ (ƛ M) ≃ ... ℰ M ...
    ℰ (M · N) ≃ ... ℰ M ... ℰ N ...

The compositionality property is not trivial because the semantics we
have defined includes three rules that are not syntax directed:
(⊥-intro), (⊔-intro), and (sub).

Next we investigate whether the denotational semantics and the
reduction semantics are equivalent. Recall that the job of a language
semantics is to describe the observable behavior of a given program
M. For the lambda calculus there are several choices that one can
make, but they usually boil down to a single bit of information:

  * divergence: the program M executes forever.
  * termination: the program M halts.

We can characterize divergence and termination in terms of reduction.

  * divergence: ¬ (M —↠ ƛ N) for any term N.
  * termination: M —↠ ƛ N for some term N.

We can also characterize divergence and termination using denotations.

  * divergence: ¬ (∅ ⊢ M ↓ v ↦ v') for any v and v'.
  * termination: ∅ ⊢ M ↓ v ↦ v' for some v and v'.

Alternatively, we can use the denotation function ℰ. 

  * divergence: ¬ (ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)) for any term N.
  * termination: ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N) for some term N.

So the question is whether the reduction semantics and denotational
semantics are equivalent.

    (∃ N. M —↠ ƛ N)  iff  (∃ N. ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N))

We address each direction of the equivalence in the second and third
chapters. In the second chapter we prove that reduction to a lambda
abstraction implies denotational equality to a lambda
abstraction. This property is called the _soundness_ in the
literature.

    M —↠ ƛ N  implies  ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)

In the third chapter we prove that denotational equality to a lambda
abstraction implies reduction to a lambda abstraction. This property
is called _adequacy_ in the literature.

    ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)  implies M —↠ ƛ N' for some N'

The proofs of these properties rely on some basic results about the
denotational semantics, which we establish in the rest of this
chapter.  We start with some lemmas about renaming, which are quite
similar to the renaming lemmas that we have seen in previous chapters.
We conclude with a proof of an important inversion lemma for the
less-than relation regarding function values.


## Renaming preserves denotations

We shall prove that renaming variables, and changing the environment
accordingly, preserves the meaning of a term. We generalize the
renaming lemma to allow the values in the new environment to be the
same or larger than the original values. This generalization is useful
in proving that reduction implies denotational equality.

As before, we need an extension lemma to handle the case where we
proceed underneath a lambda abstraction. Here, the nth function
performs lookup in the environment, analogous to Γ ∋ A.  Now suppose
that ρ is a renaming that maps variables in γ into variables with
equal or larger values in δ. This lemmas says that extending the
renaming producing a renaming (ext r) that maps (γ , v) to (δ , v).

  <a id="22866" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22868" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22768" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="22871" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#7646" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="22874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22764" class="Bound">v</a><a id="22875" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22877" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#8499" class="Function Operator">`⊑</a> <a id="22880" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="22882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22780" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="22884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#7646" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="22887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22764" class="Bound">v</a><a id="22888" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22890" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="22892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#5845" class="Function">ext</a> <a id="22896" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22796" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="22897" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="22922" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22747" class="Function">ext-nth</a> <a id="22930" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22930" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="22932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22932" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="22935" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="22938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22938" class="Bound">x</a><a id="22939" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22941" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22932" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="22946" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#22938" class="Bound">x</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We proceed by cases on the de Bruijn index n.

* If it is Z, then we just need to show that v ≡ v, which we have by refl.

* If it is S n', then the goal simplifies to nth n' γ ≡ nth (ρ n') δ,
  which is an instance of the premise.

Now for the renaming lemma. Suppose we have a renaming that maps
variables in γ into variables with the same values in δ.  If M
results in v when evaluated in environment γ, then applying the
renaming to M produces a program that results in the same value v when
evaluated in δ.

<a id="23988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#23486" class="Function">rename-pres</a> <a id="24000" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#24000" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24002" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#24002" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="24005" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24006" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#10632" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="24010" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#24010" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="24012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#24012" class="Bound">lt′</a><a id="24015" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24017" class="Symbol">=</a>
   <a id="24022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#10632" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a> <a id="24026" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#23486" class="Function">rename-pres</a> <a id="24039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#24000" class="Bound">ρ</a> <a id="24041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#24002" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="24044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#24010" class="Bound">d</a><a id="24045" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#24012" class="Bound">lt′</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof is by induction on the semantics of M.  As you can see, all
of the cases are trivial except the cases for variables and lambda.

* For a variable x, we make use of the premise to
  show that nth x γ ≡ nth (ρ x) δ.

* For a lambda abstraction, the induction hypothesis requires us to
  extend the renaming. We do so, and use the ext-nth lemma to show
  that the extended renaming maps variables to ones with equivalent
  values.


## Identity renamings and environment strengthening

We shall need a corollary of the renaming lemma that says that if M
results in v, then we can replace a value in the environment with a
larger one (a stronger one), and M still results in v. In particular,
if γ ⊢ M ↓ v and γ `⊑ δ, then δ ⊢ M ↓ v.  What does this have to do
with renaming?  It's renaming with the identity function.

The next lemma shows that renaming with an identity function is indeed
an identity function on terms. In the case of lambda abstraction, the
identity function gets extended, becoming another identity function,
but not the same one (Agda lacks extensionality).  To work around this
issue, we parameterize the proof over any function that is an
identity.

<a id="25705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25387" class="Function">rename-id</a> <a id="25715" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25716" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="25718" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25720" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="25722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="25724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25724" class="Bound">M₁</a><a id="25726" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25728" class="Bound">eq</a> <a id="25731" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25733" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#1408" class="Function">cong₂</a> <a id="25739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_·_</a> <a id="25743" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25387" class="Function">rename-id</a> <a id="25754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25728" class="Bound">eq</a><a id="25756" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25758" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25759" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25387" class="Function">rename-id</a> <a id="25769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25728" class="Bound">eq</a><a id="25771" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The identity function on variables, var-id, is an identity function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="var-id"></a><a id="25868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25868" class="Function">var-id</a> <a id="25875" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25877" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="25879" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25880" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25880" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="25882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25882" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25883" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25885" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25887" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25880" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="25890" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="25892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25882" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25893" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25895" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25898" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25880" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="25900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="25902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25882" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25903" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="25905" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25868" class="Function">var-id</a> <a id="25912" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25913" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25914" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25916" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25916" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25918" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25920" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25916" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="var-id-id"></a><a id="25923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25923" class="Function">var-id-id</a> <a id="25933" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25935" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="25937" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25938" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="25939" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25941" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25256" class="Function">is-identity</a> <a id="25955" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25956" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25938" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="25957" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25868" class="Function">var-id</a>
<a id="25966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#25923" class="Function">var-id-id</a> <a id="25976" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25978" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We can now prove environment strengthening by applying the renaming
lemma with the identity renaming, which gives us δ ⊢ rename var-id M ↓
v, and then we apply the rename-id lemma to obtain δ ⊢ M ↓ v.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Env⊑"></a><a id="26210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26210" class="Function">Env⊑</a> <a id="26215" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26217" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26219" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26220" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26220" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26221" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26223" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26224" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26224" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="26226" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#7488" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="26232" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26220" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26233" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26235" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26236" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26236" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="26238" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#7488" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="26244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26220" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26245" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26247" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26248" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="26250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26250" class="Bound">v</a><a id="26251" class="Symbol">}</a>

In the proof that substitution reflects denotations, in the case for
lambda abstraction, we use a minor variation of Env⊑, in which just
the last element of the environment gets larger.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="up-env"></a><a id="26642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26642" class="Function">up-env</a> <a id="26649" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26651" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26653" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26654" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26655" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26657" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26658" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="26660" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#7488" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="26666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26654" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="26667" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26669" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26670" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="26672" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26672" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="26674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26674" class="Bound">u₁</a> <a id="26677" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26677" class="Bound">u₂</a><a id="26679" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="26860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26802" class="Function">nth-le</a> <a id="26867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26867" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="26870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3401" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="26872" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26867" class="Bound">lt</a>
  <a id="26879" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26802" class="Function">nth-le</a> <a id="26886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26886" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="26889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26890" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="26892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#26892" class="Bound">n</a><a id="26893" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26895" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="26897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#5698" class="Function">Refl⊑</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Inversion of the less-than relation for functions

What can we deduce from knowing that a function v₁ ↦ v₁' is less than
some value v₂?  What can we deduce about v₂? The answer to this
question is called the inversion property of less-than for functions.
This question is not easy to answer because of the Dist⊑ rule, which
relates a function on the left to a pair of functions on the right.
So v₂ may include several functions that, as a group, relate to v₁ ↦
v₁'. Furthermore, because of the rules ConjR1⊑ and ConjR2⊑, there may
be other values inside v₂, such as ⊥, that have nothing to do with v₁
↦ v₁'. But in general, we can deduce that v₂ includes a collection of
functions where the join of their domains is less than v₁ and the join
of their codomains is greater than v₁'.

To precisely state and prove this inversion property, we need to
define what it means for a value to _include_ a collection of values.
We also need to define how to compute the join of their domains and
codomains.


### Value membership and inclusion

Recall that we think of a value as a set of entries with the join
operator v₁ ⊔ v₂ acting like set union. The function value v ↦ v' and
bottom value ⊥ constitute the two kinds of elements of the set.  (In
other contexts one can instead think of ⊥ as the empty set, but here
we must think of it as an element.)  We write v ∈ v' to say that v is
an element of v', as defined below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28348" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="28354" class="Number">5</a> <a id="28356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a>

<a id="_∈_"></a><a id="28361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a> <a id="28365" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="28373" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="28381" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28383" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="28387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28387" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="28389" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="28391" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a> <a id="28393" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28387" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="28397" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="28399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="28401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28401" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="28403" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="28405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28405" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="28408" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="28410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28410" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="28413" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28401" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="28417" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="28419" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28405" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="28422" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="28424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28410" class="Bound">v₂</a>
<a id="28427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28427" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="28429" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="28431" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28432" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="28435" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="28437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28437" class="Bound">v₂</a><a id="28439" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28441" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28443" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28427" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="28445" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="28447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28432" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="28450" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="28452" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28427" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="28454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="28456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28437" class="Bound">v₂</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

So we can represent a collection of values simply as a value.  We
write v₁ ⊆ v₂ to say that all the elements of v₁ are also in v₂.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28616" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="28622" class="Number">5</a> <a id="28624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">_⊆_</a>

<a id="_⊆_"></a><a id="28629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">_⊆_</a> <a id="28633" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28635" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="28641" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="28649" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28651" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="28655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28655" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="28658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="28660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28660" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="28663" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28665" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="28667" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28667" class="Bound">v₃</a><a id="28669" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28671" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28667" class="Bound">v₃</a> <a id="28676" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="28678" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28655" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="28681" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28667" class="Bound">v₃</a> <a id="28686" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="28688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28660" class="Bound">v₂</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The notions of membership and inclusion for values are closely related
to the less-than relation. They are narrower relations in that they
imply the less-than relation but not the other way around.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="∈→⊑"></a><a id="28915" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28915" class="Function">∈→⊑</a> <a id="28919" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28921" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="28923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28923" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="28926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28926" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="28929" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28931" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="28936" class="Symbol">}</a>

We shall also need some inversion principles for value inclusion.  If
the union of v₁ and v₂ is included in v₃, then of course both v₁ and
v₂ are each included in v₃.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⊔⊆-inv"></a><a id="29595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29595" class="Function">⊔⊆-inv</a> <a id="29602" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29604" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="29606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29606" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="29609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29609" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="29612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29612" class="Bound">v₃</a> <a id="29615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="29622" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="29631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29633" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29606" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="29637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="29639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29609" class="Bound">v₂</a><a id="29641" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="29645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29612" class="Bound">v₃</a>
         <a id="29657" class="Comment">---------------</a>
       <a id="29680" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29606" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="29685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="29687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29612" class="Bound">v₃</a>  <a id="29691" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a>  <a id="29694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29609" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="29697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="29699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29612" class="Bound">v₃</a>
<a id="29702" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29595" class="Function">⊔⊆-inv</a> <a id="29709" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md Operator">⟨</a> <a id="29717" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="29720" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="29721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29721" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="29770" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="29773" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In our value representation, the function value v₁ ↦ v₂ is both an
element and also a singleton set. So if v₁ ↦ v₂ is a subset of v₃,
then v₁ ↦ v₂ must be a member of v₃.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="↦⊆→∈"></a><a id="29972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29972" class="Function">↦⊆→∈</a> <a id="29977" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29979" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="29981" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29981" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="29984" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29984" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="29987" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29987" class="Bound">v₃</a> <a id="29990" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="29997" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="30004" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30006" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29981" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="30009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="30011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29984" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="30014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="30016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29987" class="Bound">v₃</a>
       <a id="30026" class="Comment">---------</a>
     <a id="30041" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29981" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="30046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="30048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29984" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="30051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="30053" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#29987" class="Bound">v₃</a>

### Function values

To identify collections of functions, we define the following two
predicates. We write Fun v₁ if v₁ is a function value, that is, if v₁
≡ v ↦ v' for some values v and v'. We write Funs v if all the elements
of v are functions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="30376" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Fun"></a><a id="30381" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30381" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="30385" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="30393" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30395" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="30399" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Fun.fun"></a><a id="30407" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30407" class="InductiveConstructor">fun</a> <a id="30411" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30413" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="30415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30415" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="30418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30418" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30420" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="30422" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="30424" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30426" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30415" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="30429" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="30431" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30418" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="30436" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30420" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="30438" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="30440" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30381" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="30446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30415" class="Bound">v₁</a>

<a id="Funs"></a><a id="30450" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30450" class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="30455" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="30463" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30465" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="30469" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30450" class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="30474" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30474" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30476" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="30478" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="30480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30480" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="30482" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="30484" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30480" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="30489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="30491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30474" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="30493" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="30495" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30381" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="30499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30480" class="Bound">v&#39;</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Of course, the value ⊥ is not a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="¬Fun⊥"></a><a id="30570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30570" class="Function">¬Fun⊥</a> <a id="30576" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30578" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="30580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30381" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="30585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a><a id="30586" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="30588" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30570" class="Function">¬Fun⊥</a> <a id="30594" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="30595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30407" class="InductiveConstructor">fun</a> <a id="30599" class="Symbol">())</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In our values-as-sets representation, our sets always include at least
one element. Thus, if all the elements are functions, there is at
least one that is a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Funs∈"></a><a id="30796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30796" class="Function">Funs∈</a> <a id="30802" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30804" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="30806" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30806" class="Bound">v₁</a><a id="30808" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Domains and codomains

Returning to our goal, the inversion principle for less-than a
function, we want to show that v₁ ↦ v₁' ⊑ v₂ implies that v₂ includes
a set of function values such that the join of their domains is less
than v₁ and the join of their codomains is greater than v₁'.

To this end we define the following dom and cod functions.  Given some
value v (that represents a set of entries), dom v returns the join of
their domains and cod v returns the join of their codomains.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="dom"></a><a id="31592" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31592" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="31596" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31598" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31599" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31601" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31603" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="31608" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a>
<a id="31618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31592" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="31622" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>  <a id="31625" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="31629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31592" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="31633" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31634" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="31638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31638" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="31640" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31642" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31644" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31634" class="Bound">v</a>
<a id="31646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31592" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="31650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31651" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="31655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31655" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="31657" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31659" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31592" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="31665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31651" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31667" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="31669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31592" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="31673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31655" class="Bound">v&#39;</a>

<a id="cod"></a><a id="31677" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31677" class="Function">cod</a> <a id="31681" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31683" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31684" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31686" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="31693" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31695" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a>
<a id="31703" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31677" class="Function">cod</a> <a id="31707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>  <a id="31710" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4121" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a>
<a id="31714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31677" class="Function">cod</a> <a id="31718" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31719" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="31723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31723" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="31725" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31727" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31723" class="Bound">v&#39;</a>
<a id="31732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31677" class="Function">cod</a> <a id="31736" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31737" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31737" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="31741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31741" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="31743" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31745" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31677" class="Function">cod</a> <a id="31751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31737" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31753" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="31755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31677" class="Function">cod</a> <a id="31759" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31741" class="Bound">v&#39;</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We need just one property each for dom and cod.  Given a collection of
functions represented by value v, and an entry v₁ ↦ v₂ in v, we know
that v₁ is included in the domain of v.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="↦∈→⊆dom"></a><a id="31968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31968" class="Function">↦∈→⊆dom</a> <a id="31976" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31978" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="31980" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31980" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="31982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31982" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="31985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31985" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="31988" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31990" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="31995" class="Symbol">}</a>

Regarding cod, suppose we have a collection of functions represented
by v, but all of them are just copies of v₁ ↦ v₂.  Then the cod v is
included in v₂.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⊆↦→cod⊆"></a><a id="32538" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#32538" class="Function">⊆↦→cod⊆</a> <a id="32546" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32548" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="32550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#32550" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="32552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#32552" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="32555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#32555" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="32558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="32565" class="Symbol">}</a>

class="Bound">z</a><a id="32846" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="32849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#32813" class="Bound">y</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

With the dom and cod functions in hand, we can make precise the
conclusion of the inversion principle for functions, which we package
into the following predicate named factor. We say that v₁ ↦ v₁'
_factors_ v₂ into v₂' if v₂' is a included in v₂, if v₂' contains only
functions, its domain is less than v₁, and its codomain is greater
than v₁'.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="factor"></a><a id="33223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33223" class="Function">factor</a> <a id="33230" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33232" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33233" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33233" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="33236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33238" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="33243" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33245" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33247" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33248" class="Bound">v₂&#39;</a> <a id="33252" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33254" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="33259" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33261" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33263" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33264" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33264" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="33267" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="33274" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33276" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33278" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33279" class="Bound">v₁&#39;</a> <a id="33283" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="33290" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33292" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33294" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="33298" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33223" class="Function">factor</a> <a id="33305" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33305" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="33308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33308" class="Bound">v₂&#39;</a> <a id="33312" href="{% endraw %}{{ class="Bound">v₁&#39;</a> <a id="33319" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="33321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30450" class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="33326" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="33332" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33308" class="Bound">v₂&#39;</a> <a id="33336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="33338" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33305" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="33341" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="33343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31592" class="Function">dom</a> <a id="33347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33308" class="Bound">v₂&#39;</a> <a id="33351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4466" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="33353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33312" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="33356" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="33358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33315" class="Bound">v₁&#39;</a> <a id="33362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4466" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="33364" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#31677" class="Function">cod</a> <a id="33368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#33308" class="Bound">v₂&#39;</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We prove the inversion principle for functions by induction on the
derivation of the less-than relation. To make the induction hypothesis
stronger, we broaden the premise to v₁ ⊑ v₂ (instead of v₁ ↦ v₁' ⊑
v₂), and strengthen the conclusion to say that for _every_ function
value w₁ ↦ w₁' ∈ v₁, we have that w₁ ↦ w₁' factors v₂ into v₂'.

### Inversion of less-than for functions, the case for Trans⊑

The crux of the proof is the case for Trans⊑.

    v₁ ⊑ u   u ⊑ v₂
    --------------- (Trans⊑)
        v₁ ⊑ v₂

By the induction hypothesis for v₁ ⊑ u, we know
that w₁ ↦ w₁' factors u into u', for some value u',
so we have Funs u' and u' ⊆ u.
By the induction hypothesis for u ⊑ v₂, we know
that for any u₁ ↦ u₂ ∈ u, u₁ ↦ u₂ factors v₂ into v₂'.
With these facts in hand, we proceed by induction on u'
to prove that (dom u') ↦ (cod u') factors v₂ into v₂'.
We discuss each case of the proof in the text below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-inv-trans"></a><a id="34310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#34310" class="Function">sub-inv-trans</a> <a id="34324" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34326" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="34328" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#34328" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="34331" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#34331" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="34334" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#34334" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="34336" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34338" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="34343" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="35225" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="35231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35231" class="Function">fv₂&#39;</a> <a id="35236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35238" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35239" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="35242" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="35249" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35251" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35239" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="35256" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="35258" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#34963" class="Bound">v₂₁&#39;</a> <a id="35263" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="35265" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35239" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="35268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="35270" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35034" class="Bound">v₂₂&#39;</a> <a id="35275" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30381" class="Datatype">Fun</a> <a id="35281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35239" class="Bound">v&#39;</a>
          <a id="35294" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35231" class="Function">fv₂&#39;</a> <a id="35299" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35300" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35300" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="35302" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35304" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35305" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="35310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35310" class="Bound">x</a><a id="35311" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35313" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="35315" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#34972" class="Bound">fu21&#39;</a> <a id="35321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35310" class="Bound">x</a>
          <a id="35333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35231" class="Function">fv₂&#39;</a> <a id="35338" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35339" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35339" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="35341" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35343" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35344" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="35349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35349" class="Bound">y</a><a id="35350" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35352" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="35354" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35043" class="Bound">fu22&#39;</a> <a id="35360" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35349" class="Bound">y</a>
          <a id="35372" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35372" class="Function">v₂&#39;⊆v₂</a> <a id="35379" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35381" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35382" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35382" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="35384" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="35391" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35393" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35382" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="35397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="35399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#34963" class="Bound">v₂₁&#39;</a> <a id="35404" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="35406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35382" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="35408" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="35410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35034" class="Bound">v₂₂&#39;</a> <a id="35415" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35382" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="35419" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28361" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="35421" class="Bound">v₂</a>
          <a id="35434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35372" class="Function">v₂&#39;⊆v₂</a> <a id="35441" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35442" class="Bound">C</a><a id="35443" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35445" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35446" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="35451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35451" class="Bound">x</a><a id="35452" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35454" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="35456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#34982" class="Bound">v₂₁&#39;⊆v₂</a> <a id="35464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35451" class="Bound">x</a>
          <a id="35476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35372" class="Function">v₂&#39;⊆v₂</a> <a id="35483" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35484" class="Bound">C</a><a id="35485" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35488" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="35493" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35493" class="Bound">y</a><a id="35494" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35496" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="35498" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35053" class="Bound">v₂₂&#39;⊆v₂</a> <a id="35506" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#35493" class="Bound">y</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Suppose u' ≡ ⊥. Then we have a contradiction because
  it is not the case that Fun ⊥.

* Suppose u' ≡ u₁' ↦ u₂'. Then u₁' ↦ u₂' ∈ u and we can apply the
  premise (the induction hypothesis from u ⊑ v₂) to obtain that
  u₁' ↦ u₂' factors of v₂ into v₂'. This case is complete because
  dom u' ≡ u₁' and cod u' ≡ u₂'.
  
* Suppose u' ≡ u₁' ⊔ u₂'. Then we have u₁' ⊆ u and u₂' ⊆ u. We also  
  have Funs u₁' and Funs u₂', so we can apply the induction hypothesis
  for both u₁' and u₂'. So there exists values v₂₁' and v₂₂' such that
  (dom u₁') ↦ (cod u₁') factors u into v₂₁' and
  (dom u₂') ↦ (cod u₂') factors u into v₂₂'.
  We will show that (dom u) ↦ (cod u) factors u into (v₂₁' ⊔ v₂₂').
  So we need to show that
  
        dom (v₂₁' ⊔ v₂₂') ⊑ dom (u₁' ⊔ u₂')
        cod (u₁' ⊔ u₂') ⊑ cod (v₂₁' ⊔ v₂₂')
  
  But those both follow directly from the factoring of
  u into v₂₁' and v₂₂', using the monotonicity of ⊔ with respect to ⊑.
  

### Inversion of less-than for functions

We come to the proof of the main lemma concerning the inversion of
less-than for functions. We show that if v₁ ⊑ v₂, then for any w₁ ↦
w₁' ∈ v₁, we can factor v₂ into v₂' according to w₁ ↦ w₁'. We proceed
by induction on the derivation of v₁ ⊑ v₂, and describe each case in
the text after the Agda proof.

    <a id="38365" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38366" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.</a><a id="38367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38312" class="DottedPattern Bound">v₂₁</a><a id="38370" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38372" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="38373" class="DottedPattern Symbol">.(</a><a id="38375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38319" class="DottedPattern Bound">v₂₂</a> <a id="38379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="DottedPattern InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="38381" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38325" class="DottedPattern Bound">v₂₃</a><a id="38384" class="DottedPattern Symbol">)</a><a id="38385" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="38387" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="38392" class="Symbol">=</a>

  <a id="38475" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="38481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38481" class="Function">f</a> <a id="38483" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30450" class="Function">Funs</a> <a id="38490" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38312" class="Bound">v₂₁</a> <a id="38495" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="38497" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38319" class="Bound">v₂₂</a> <a id="38501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="38503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38312" class="Bound">v₂₁</a> <a id="38507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="38509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38325" class="Bound">v₂₃</a><a id="38512" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="38522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38481" class="Function">f</a> <a id="38524" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38525" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="38530" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38530" class="Bound">x</a><a id="38531" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38533" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="38535" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30407" class="InductiveConstructor">fun</a> <a id="38539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38530" class="Bound">x</a>
        <a id="38549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38481" class="Function">f</a> <a id="38551" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38552" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="38557" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38557" class="Bound">y</a><a id="38558" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38560" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="38562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#30407" class="InductiveConstructor">fun</a> <a id="38566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38557" class="Bound">y</a>
        <a id="38576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38576" class="Function">g</a> <a id="38578" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="38580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38581" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38312" class="Bound">v₂₁</a> <a id="38585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="38593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38325" class="Bound">v₂₃</a><a id="38602" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#28629" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="38606" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38607" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38312" class="Bound">v₂₁</a> <a id="38611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="38613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38319" class="Bound">v₂₂</a> <a id="38617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4163" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="38619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38312" class="Bound">v₂₁</a> <a id="38623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="38625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38325" class="Bound">v₂₃</a><a id="38628" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="38638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38576" class="Function">g</a> <a id="38640" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38641" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="38646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38646" class="Bound">x</a><a id="38647" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38649" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="38651" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="38656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38646" class="Bound">x</a>
        <a id="38666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38576" class="Function">g</a> <a id="38668" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="38669" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="38674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38674" class="Bound">y</a><a id="38675" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="38677" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="38679" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="38684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#38674" class="Bound">y</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let w₁ w₁' be arbitrary values.

* Case (Bot⊑). So v₁ ≡ ⊥. We have w₁ ↦ w₁' ∈ ⊥, but that is impossible.

* Case (ConjL⊑).

        v₁₁ ⊑ v₂   v₁₂ ⊑ v₂
        -------------------
        v₁₁ ⊔ v₁₂ ⊑ v₂

  Given that w₁ ↦ w₁' ∈ v₁₁ ⊔ v₁₂, there are two subcases to consider.

  * Subcase w₁ ↦ w₁' ∈ v₁₁. We conclude by the induction
    hypothesis for v₁₁ ⊑ v₂.
  
  * Subcase w₁ ↦ w₁' ∈ v₁₂. We conclude by the induction hypothesis
    for v₁₂ ⊑ v₂.

* Case (ConjR1⊑).

        v₁ ⊑ v₂₁
        --------------
        v₁ ⊑ v₂₁ ⊔ v₂₂

  Given that w₁ ↦ w₁' ∈ v₁, the induction hypothesis for v₁ ⊑ v₂₁
  gives us that w₁ ↦ w₁' factors v₂₁ into v₂₁' for some v₂₁'.
  To show that w₁ ↦ w₁' also factors (v₂₁ ⊔ v₂₂) into v₂₁',
  we just need to show that v₂₁' ⊆ v₂₁ ⊔ v₂₂, but that follows
  directly from v₂₁' ⊆ v₂₁.

* Case (ConjR2⊑). This case follows by reasoning similar to
  the case for (ConjR1⊑).

* Case (Trans⊑). 

        v₁ ⊑ u   u ⊑ v₂
        ---------------
            v₁ ⊑ v₂
        
  By the induction hypothesis for v₁ ⊑ u, we know
  that w₁ ↦ w₁' factors u into u', for some value u',
  so we have Funs u' and u' ⊆ u.
  By the induction hypothesis for u ⊑ v₂, we know
  that for any u₁ ↦ u₂ ∈ u, u₁ ↦ u₂ factors v₂ into v₂'.
  Now we apply the lemma sub-inv-trans, which gives us
  some v₂' such that (dom u') ↦ (cod u') factors v₂ into v₂'.
  We show that w₁ ↦ w₁' also factors v₂ into v₂'.
  From dom v₂' ⊑ dom u' and dom u' ⊑ w₁, we have dom v₂' ⊑ w₁.
  From w₁' ⊑ cod u' and cod u' ⊑ cod v₂', we have w₁' ⊑ cod v₂',
  and this case is complete.

* Case (Fun⊑).

        v₂₁ ⊑ v₁₁  v₁₂ ⊑ v₂₂
        ---------------------
        v₁₁ ↦ v₁₂ ⊑ v₂₁ ↦ v₂₂

  Given that w₁ ↦ w₁' ∈ v₁₁ ↦ v₁₂, we have w₁ ≡ v₁₁ and w₁' ≡ v₁₂.
  We show that v₁₁ ↦ v₁₂ factors v₂₁ ↦ v₂₂ into itself.
  We need to show that dom (v₂₁ ↦ v₂₂) ⊑ v₁₁ and v₁₂ ⊑ cod (v₂₁ ↦ v₂₂),
  but that is equivalent to our premises v₂₁ ⊑ v₁₁ and v₁₂ ⊑ v₂₂.

* Case (Dist⊑).

        ---------------------------------------------
        v₂₁ ↦ (v₂₂ ⊔ v₂₃) ⊑ (v₂₁ ↦ v₂₂) ⊔ (v₂₁ ↦ v₂₃)

  Given that w₁ ↦ w₁' ∈ v₂₁ ↦ (v₂₂ ⊔ v₂₃), we have w₁ ≡ v₂₁
  and w₁' ≡ v₂₂ ⊔ v₂₃.
  We show that v₂₁ ↦ (v₂₂ ⊔ v₂₃) factors (v₂₁ ↦ v₂₂) ⊔ (v₂₁ ↦ v₂₃) into itself.
  We have v₂₁ ⊔ v₂₁ ⊑ v₂₁, and also
  v₂₂ ⊔ v₂₃ ⊑ v₂₂ ⊔ v₂₃, so the proof is complete.


We conclude this section with two corollaries of the sub-inv lemma.
First, we have the following property that is convenient to use in
later proofs. We specialize the premise to just (v₁ ↦ v₁') ⊑ v₂
and we modify the conclusion to say that for every
w ↦ w' ∈ v₂', we have w ⊑ v₁.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-inv-fun"></a><a id="41305" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#41305" class="Function">sub-inv-fun</a> <a id="41317" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41319" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="41321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#41321" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="41324" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#41324" class="Bound">v₁&#39;</a> <a id="41328" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#41328" class="Bound">v₂</a> <a id="41331" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="41333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4101" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="41338" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="41344" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="41346" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="41347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#41321" class="Bound">v₁</a> <a id="41350" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4133" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="41352" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#41324" class="Bound">v₁&#39;</a><a id="41355" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="41357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#4466" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="41359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denot.md %}{% raw %}#41328" class="Bound">v₂</a>

The second corollary is the inversion rule that one would expect for
less-than with functions on the left and right-hand sides.

## Notes

[JGS: todo: reorganize these notes for the new chapters]

The denotational semantics presented in this chapter is an example of
a *filter model* (Barendregt, Coppo, Dezani-Ciancaglini, 1983). Filter
models use type systems with intersection types to precisely
characterize runtime behavior (Coppo, Dezani-Ciancaglini, and Salle,
1979). The notation that we use in this chapter is not that of type
systems and intersection types, but the Value data type is isomorphic
to types (↦ is →, ⊔ is ∧, ⊥ is ⊤), the ⊑ relation is the inverse of
subtyping <:, and the evaluation relation ρ ⊢ M ↓ v is isomorphic to a
type system. Write Γ instead of ρ, A instead of v, and replace ↓ with : and
one has Γ ⊢ M : A.  By varying the definition of subtyping and
using different choices of type atoms, intersection type systems can
provide semantics for many different untyped λ calculi, from full beta
to the lazy and call-by-value calculi (Alessi, Barbanera, and
Dezani-Ciancaglini, 2006) (Rocca and Paolini, 2004).  The denotational
semantics in this chapter corresponds to the BCD system (Barendregt,
Coppo, Dezani-Ciancaglini, 1983).  Part 3 of the book _Lambda Calculus
with Types_ describes a framework for intersection type systems that
enables results similar to the ones in this chapter, but for the
entire family of intersection type systems (Barendregt, Dekkers, and
Statman, 2013).

The two ideas of using finite tables to represent functions and of
relaxing table lookup to enable self application first appeared in a
technical report by Gordon Plotkin (1972) and are later described in
an article in Theoretical Computer Science (Plotkin 1993).  In that
work, the inductive definition of Value is a bit different than the
one we use:
 
    Value = C + ℘f(Value) × ℘f(Value)
 
where C is a set of constants and ℘f means finite powerset.  The pairs
in ℘f(Value) × ℘f(Value) represent input-output mappings, just as in
this chapter. The finite powersets are used to enable a function table
to appear in the input and in the output. These differences amount to
changing where the recursion appears in the definition of Value.
Plotkin's model is an example of a _graph model_ of the untyped lambda
calculus (Barendregt, 1984). In a graph model, the semantics is
presented as a function from programs and environments to (possibly
infinite) sets of values. The semantics in this chapter is instead
defined as a relation, but set-valued functions are isomorphic to
relations. We choose to present the semantics as a relation because
the functional approach requires a kind of existential quantifier that
is not present in Agda.

[PLW: What kind of existential is required?]

Dana Scott's ℘(ω) (1976) and Engeler's B(A) (1981) are two more
examples of graph models. Both use the following inductive definition
of Value.
 
    Value = C + ℘f(Value) × Value
 
The use of Value instead of ℘f(Value) in the output does not restrict
expressiveness compared to Plotkin's model because the semantics use
sets of values and a pair of sets (V, V') can be represented as a set
of pairs { (V, v') | v' ∈ V' }.  In Scott's ℘(ω), the above values are
mapped to and from the natural numbers using a kind of Godel encoding.


## References

* Intersection Types and Lambda Models.  Fabio Alessi, Franco
  Barbanera, and Mariangiola Dezani-Ciancaglini, Theoretical
  Compututer Science, vol. 355, pages 108-126, 2006.

* The Lambda Calculus. H.P. Barendregt, 1984.

* A filter lambda model and the completeness of type assignment.  Henk
  Barendregt, Mario Coppo, and Mariangiola Dezani-Ciancaglini, Journal
  of Symbolic Logic, vol. 48, pages 931-940, 1983.

* Lambda Calculus with Types. Henk Barendregt, Wil Dekkers, and
  Richard Statman, Cambridge University Press, Perspectives in Logic,
  2013.

* Functional characterization of some semantic equalities inside
  λ-calculus. Mario Coppo, Mariangiola Dezani-Ciancaglini, and Patrick
  Salle, in Sixth Colloquium on Automata, Languages and Programming.
  Springer, pages 133--146, 1979.

* Algebras and combinators. Erwin Engeler, Algebra Universalis,
  vol. 13, pages 389-392, 1981.

* A Set-Theoretical Definition of Application. Gordon D. Plotkin,
  University of Edinburgh, Technical Report MIP-R-95, 1972.

* Set-theoretical and other elementary models of the λ-calculus.
  Gordon D. Plotkin, Theoretical Computer Science, vol. 121,
  pages 351-409, 1993.

* The Parametric Lambda Calculus. Simona Ronchi Della Rocca and Luca
  Paolini, Springer, 2004.

* Data Types as Lattices. Dana Scott, SIAM Journal on Computing,
  vol. 5, pages 522-587, 1976.
